<date>1511654933539</date><rating>3<//rating>< Review>
Great location, friendly staff, very clean (shout out to the cleaning crew!) but for a new gym it's missing or has low amounts of key equipment. There's only two squat racks inside and a gym block outside (which you can put squat bars on). One hex bar (outside). Low weight standing calf machine (under 300 lbs). Two flat benches. Ultimately this gym has enough to work out in, but it's difficult if you are into powerlifting, especially during the busy times as there just is not enough equipment, or low weight machines. As a result the gym is passable, but you'll need to work out during non peak hours if you want to use the equipment listed above, and don't even think about trying to get a circuit in. Also fair warning the first month of billing they will tag on an additional $39.99 charge to keep your current rate locked in gym price, so essentially they charge you to not charge you more! Lol, maybe I'm naive because I'm from the Midwest. One other issue I had was they didn't have my pass tied to my account. As a result when I asked them for my attendance they were like whoops! Then my work which requires attendance to gyms for reimbursement (health bucks), wasn't able to see my attendance (I asked the EOS supervisor for an email explaining, and she sent it, but was not satisfactory for my work). As a result I lost out on the $125 fit bucks for that quarter. :/ in my opinion this gym has potential, but it's untapped in its current state, and I'm giving it a slight pass since it's a newer gym.<//Review>

I just want to say thanks to Manuel, Mike and the rest of the team at this location.  They came to me from a referral and I needed major help with a massive oil leak I had on my 1999 Jetta.  They took it in on a Saturday, got to it in a timely manner and gave me a breakdown of the possibilities and estimate.  We waited for the hard-to-find German parts to come in and they got to the car right away.  I got a call with the news that they discovered it might only be an o-ring that would need to be replaced and not the whole oil filter bracket.  They replaced the o-ring, reinstalled the existing bracket and...it worked!  They returned the ordered part, saving me almost $300 and charged me only the cost of the o-ring labor and oil. When engine warning lights all came on and started to randomly flash I headed to Midas. The engine died as I rolled into the parking lot. Mike quickly responded, opened the hood, assigned a mechanic to trouble shoot the problem.  Within thirty minutes the diagnosis was: failed alternator and belt tensioner. The parts were in stock. <Review>They specialize in troubleshooting, inspection, evaluation, and explanations.
Automotive technicians that ACTUALLY troubleshoot, inspect, and offer their recommendations as well as the reasoning behind their recommendations. Every visit (four times, I think), either repair or routine maintenance, has had long term and lasting positive results down the road. 170k miles down and another 200k or more to go, I hope, with their TLC maintenance.
A couple experiences.  My transmission was shifting rough around 30 mph.  I took it to a local transmission specialist shop.  They "shotgun" troubleshot the problem from the desk and just swapped out some solenoids within the transmission.  I didn't want them touching my car again so I found Midas in Visalia.  They diagnosed the issue to one of the three speed sensors in the drive line being faulty.  Swapped it out and it shifts much smoother now.  I had an A/C fan shutdown issue at certain driving conditions.  They troubleshot it COMPLETELY and told me exactly which part is bad, how it is likely "broken", how cheap the part is, and how labor intensive (expensive $) it'd be to dig the part out of the dash.  The way they explain their findings have always left me with a feeling that I understand the condition of my car a LOT better than any other shop I've ever been to.  Shop around for prices if you want (car repairs aren't cheap), but personally, I find it difficult to put a price on the piece of mind I get here.</Review>< gmap_id>
